ha ha ha ha ... defeat the ^tin robot^ to get a ^token^!
hi buzz! please find my ^five^ missing ^sheep^. when you find them come back and see me for a pizza planet ^token^.
you found my ^sheep^ buzz! thank you, here is your pizza planet ^token^.
hi buzz! i challenge you to a race! we will race ^3^ laps around the car. if you beat me, i will give you a pizza planet ^token.^ get ready to race 3... 2... 1...
if you press the fire button you can attack with your laser. if you press the spin button you can attack with your spin attack. hold down the button to charge up the attack. your spin attack can deflect objects that are fired at you.
if you jump at a horizontal bar you will swing around it. press jump when you have left the bar to jump farther and higher.
you can change camera mode using the pause menu. active camera will always try and turn to view buzz from behind. passive camera will not turn. the l and r trigger buttons turn the ^camera^ in ^passive^ mode and turn ^buzz^ in ^active^ mode.
if you see the ^push^ icon you can run into the object and push it out of the way. 
if you press the jump button once and then press it again you can do an extended jump. use it to get onto the table and then to reach the open drawer.
you can grab onto poles. when you are holding on you can push up and down to move up and down the pole. you can press left and right to turn on the pole. press jump to let go of the pole.
you can jump onto zip lines to slide down them. press jump to let go of the line.
you can target your laser by using your visor view. press the y button to activate the view. then press the r and l trigger buttons to swap between visible targets, then press fire to use your laser. use it to shoot the catches holding up the side of the crib.
you can foot ^stomp^ where you see the ^stomp^ icon by pressing jump and then pressing ^spin^ while you are in the air. this will activate switches and catapults and will also act as an attack.
hey buzz! you need a ^cosmic shield^ to cross the ^green sludge^. find my missing ^ear^ and i will let you use the ^cosmic shield^!
wow! thanks buzz! in return for finding my ^ear^ i will let you use the ^cosmic shield^. it will only protect you from harm for a little while so make sure you use it wisely.
the ^cosmic shield^ will only protect you from harm for a little while so make sure you use it wisely.
^hamm^ is sitting on the sofa in the living room.
^bo peep^ has lost her sheep. she is on the table in the ^kitchen^.
^r.c. car^ is waiting to race you around the garage. he is through the hole in the door downstairs.
you can move the boxes on the shelf in the ^basement^ to get to the token on the shelf. it is easier with the ^cosmic shield^. mr. potato head will let you use it, if you find his ^ear^ for him.
the ^tin robot^ boss is in the attic above us. you can reach the attic by climbing the plant and then the rope.
i need your help, space ranger! ^five^ of my ^troops^ are lost. look for the ^flares^ they are using to signal to you. locate them for me and i will give you a pizza planet ^token^!
great job locating the ^troops^! here is your pizza planet ^token^.
ha ha ha ha ... defeat the ^zurg kite^ to get a ^token^!
hi buzz! i challenge you to a race! we will race ^3^ laps around the garden. if you beat me, i will give you a pizza planet ^token.^ get ready to race 3... 2... 1...
^hamm^ is on the first branch of the ^tree^. climb the ^swing set^ to get to him.
^sarge^ has lost his troops. he is on the steps of andy's house. the troops are using ^flares^ to help you find them. 
^r.c. car^ is waiting to race you around the garden. i better warn you though you won't be able to beat him without your ^rocket jet boots^ and your ^rocket jet boots^ aren't available until you help ^mr. potato head^ on another level.
you can inflate the ^rubber duck^ to get to the token over the ^swimming pool^.
the ^kite boss^ is at the top of the tree. hey buzz, you can find a rope on the way up! jump onto it and it will fall to the ground. that way you can quickly get back into the tree.
the soldier will surrender if you quickly ^stomp^ on the ^molehills^ that he is near.
if you can mix the the paint to match the colors on the wall you will get a pizza planet ^token^.
hi buzz! if you find my ^five^ missing ^little tikes^ and come back and find me, i will give you a pizza planet ^token^.
thanks for finding my ^little tikes^ buzz! here is a pizza planet ^token^!
ha ha ha ha ... defeat the ^jackhammer^ boss to get a pizza planet ^token^! i hope you have the ^disk launcher^!
hi buzz! if you can find ^five^ missing ^wrenches^ and bring them to me in time, i will give you a pizza planet ^token^!
hurry up buzz! you still have ^wrenches^ to find!
well done buzz! you have found all the ^wrenches^! here is your pizza planet ^token^!
hi buzz! you need a ^disk launcher^ to defeat the angry ^jackhammer^ boss. find my missing ^eye^, i will give you the ^disk launcher^!
wow! thanks buzz! in return for finding my ^eye^ i will let you use the ^disk launcher^. it should help you defeat the toughest enemies!
the ^disk launcher^ will help you defeat the toughest enemies!
i think i saw hamm over by the ^wheelbarrow^.
the ^foreman^ has lost his little tike workers. he is over by the ^trailer^.
^slinky^ is right under the girders. he has a ^challenge^ for you!
there is a paint mixing puzzle to solve in the ^trailer^!
the ^jackhammer^ boss is at the top of the girders. i better warn you though, you need to help ^mr. potato head^ find his eye to get the ^disk launcher^ to defeat the ^jackhammer^ boss.
ha ha ha ha ... defeat the ^ clown top^ boss to get a pizza planet ^token^!
hi buzz! i have lost all my ^baby ducklings^! if you can find all ^five^ of them and come and see me, i will give you a pizza planet ^token^.
thanks for finding my ^baby ducklings^ buzz! here is a pizza planet ^token^!
howdy buzz! if you can bring me ^five^ bones before you run out of time, i will give you a pizza planet ^token^.
quick! you need to find more bones!
well done! you found all of my bones! here is your pizza planet ^token^!
i saw ^hamm^ in the market place near an ^umbrella^.
the ^mother duck^ has lost her ^ducklings^. she is near the central drain.
^slinky^ has a ^challenge^ for you. he is on the island in the middle of the ^gully^ over this fence.
there is a ^token^ on the table in the market place. you need to float over to it on a ^balloon^.
the ^clown top^ boss is on the roof of the apartment building. you need a ^grappling hook^ to climb up. help ^mr. potato head^ on another level to open the ^grappling hook^.
hi buzz! you need ^rocket boots^ to cross over to the shopping cart. find my missing ^arm^, i will let you use the ^rocket boots^!
wow! thanks buzz! thanks for finding my ^arm^. now you can use the ^rocket boots^. they give you great speed for a short amount of time. they're great for racing around with!
the ^rocket boots^ give you great speed for a short amount of time. they're great for racing around with!
ha ha ha ha ... defeat the ^dinosaur^ boss to get a pizza planet ^token^!
hi buzz! if you find my ^five^ missing ^chicks^ and come back and find me, i will give you a pizza planet ^token^.
thanks for finding my ^chicks^ buzz! here is a pizza planet ^token^!
if you can get to my hatching ^egg^ in time you can keep the ^chick^ that you find in it! come back and see me after you have got the ^chick^!
hurry up, buzz! the ^egg^ is still hatching!
this time the egg will hatch quicker but there is a ^token^ inside it! get to it in time and you can keep the ^token^!
i saw ^hamm^ on the table in the ^office^.
the ^chicken^ has lost her ^chicks^. she is just past the ^bike^ section. buzz, one of the ^chicks^ is on the top of the boxes in this room! you'll need the ^hover boots^ to reach it and ^mr. potato head^ won't give you ^hover boots^ until later.
the ^rooster^ is at the end of the ^hall^ by the office. he has some ^challenges^ for you!
there is a ^token^ on top of the cabinets in the ^office^. you need to open up the ^locked^ drawers to get to it. try using the ^disk launcher^! if you haven't unlocked it yet, go see ^mr. potato head^ in the ^construction yard^ level.
the ^dinosaur^ boss is through a tunnel to the ^left^ of here.
the ^hay bale ride^ will buck you over to the ^chick^ on the gumball machine but it will stop if you leave the area. unlock the ^rocket boots^ and jet over to the shopping cart to solve this puzzle.
hey space ranger! return to your ship immediately!... defeat the ^buzz lightyear buggy^ boss to get a pizza planet ^token^!
hi buzz! if you find my ^five^ missing ^aliens^ and come back and find me, i will give you a pizza planet ^token^.
thanks for finding my ^aliens^ buzz! here is a pizza planet ^token^!
hi buzz! if you can beat me to the end of the ^zipline^ course i will give you a pizza planet ^token^!
i saw ^hamm^ at the end of the ^laser battle zone^.
the ^mothership^ has returned for the ^aliens^. she is waiting near a pile of boxes.
there is a ^flying saucer^ that wants to challenge you to a ^race^. it is waiting at the start of the ^zipline^ course.
there is a ^token^ in the claw machine next to you. stomp the button to grab the ^token^.
the ^buzz lightyear buggy^ boss is in a room that can only be reached by climbing the space ^mobile^ in the central area.
^stomp^ button once to put claw in motion from side to side. ^stomp^ button again to put it in motion from front to back. when claw is centered over ^token^ foot ^stomp^ one last time to grab it. collect your prize below!
ha ha ha ha ... defeat the ^spider gunro^ boss to get a pizza planet ^token^!

wow! thanks buzz! in return for finding my ^foot^ i will let you use the ^grappling hook^. you can aim at the special targets in visor view using the trigger buttons and you can launch the hook by pressing fire!

hi buzz! follow the ^token^ to the ^bottom^ of the shaft where you can collect it unless you run out of time.

if you line up the ^wire^ you will open the ^door^ and activate the ^elevators^.

the ^spider gunro^ boss is in a room above the elevator shafts.

you can get to the token on top of the ^train bed^ if you solve the train puzzle. you need to get the train to stop on the dead end track. you can change the track points using the yellow switches.
the ^gunslinger^ boss is in the woody's roundup set in the ^trophy room^.
^stomp^ the buttons to raise and lower the water level. the button in the bottom of the tub will drain all the water. the other buttons will raise the water to their level. 
^stomp^ the buttons to change the track points and make the train switch tracks. get the train to go onto the dead end track so that you can push the box to the ^train bed^ to reach the pizza planet ^token^.
 !"#$%BCDEFHIJKLMO
ha ha ha ha ... defeat the ^prospector^ boss to get a pizza planet ^token^!
hi buzz! if you can bring me ^five^ weights before you run out of time, i will give you a pizza planet ^token^.
quick! you need to find more weights!
well done! you have found all of my weights! here is your pizza planet ^token^!
hi buzz! if you can find ^five little tike passengers^ for my next flight i will give you a pizza planet ^token^.
thanks for finding my ^little tike passengers^ buzz! here is a pizza planet ^token^!
mmm.. mumpf! mmmmu mo mmmme ^hover boots^ mmmm mub ^mouth^ mmmum mi mo mmmump!
wow! thanks buzz! in return for finding my ^mouth^ i will let you use the ^hover boots^. you can float higher by holding down the ^jump^ button and you can float lower by letting go of the ^jump^ button.
with the ^hover boots^ you can float higher by holding down the ^jump^ button and you can float lower by letting go of the ^jump^ button.
^hamm^ is on the shelf at the end of the x-ray room.
the ^little tike pilot^ has lost his passengers. he is in the repair hangar.
^rocky gilbraltor^ has a ^challenge^ for you. he is on the floor of the conveyor belt room.
you can get to the ^token^ on top of the broken plane using the ^hover boots^. mr. potato head has them near the stack of luggage.
the ^prospector^ boss is on the conveyor belt at the top of the luggage stack. you need the ^hover boots^ to reach him.
ha ha ha ha ... defeat the ^blacksmith^ boss to get a pizza planet ^token^!
hi buzz! if you can reach the end of this path without ^jumping^ or touching the ^green^ slime, i will give you a pizza planet ^token^.
quick! you can still reach the token!
hi buzz! i have lost ^five^ pieces of ^luggage^. if you can find them for me, i will give you a pizza planet ^token^.
thanks for finding my ^luggage^ buzz! here is a pizza planet ^token^!
i think i saw ^hamm^ in zone ^5^.
the ^airport little tike^ has lost his ^luggage^. he is in zone ^3^.
^slinky^ has a ^challenge^ for you. he is in the middle of the airport next to the central pole. by the way, you can jump on the plane from the central pole.
there is a ^token^ being carried by the ^helicopter^. signal the ^helicopter^ to land by solving the ^lights^ puzzle in zone ^1^. you can use the ^zipline^ at the end of this trolley to reach the puzzle area.
the ^blacksmith^ boss is on the roof of the building in zone ^7^. he is near the radar tower. try and reach it by running down the wings of the ^plane^.
use the ^buttons^ to change the bottom row of lights to match the top row of lights. the puzzle will reset if you take more than ^3^ tries. if you complete the puzzle the helicopter will move down so that you can reach the pizza planet ^token^.
